In the following passage some words have been deleted. Fill in the blanks with the help of the
alternatives given. Select the most appropriate option for each blank.
Discipline is doing any work with rules and regulations. It is (1)______ misunderstood as a
restriction to freedom but it makes our life organized. Discipline is a (2)______ for students
and people in different professions. A disciplined person always (3)______ in each and every
field of life. Disciplined people (4)______ a disciplined society and a powerful nation.
Discipline should not be (5)______ upon the people, rather it should come from within.

restriction to freedom but it makes our life organized. Discipline is a (2)______ for students

Q.1 Given below are four jumbled sentences. Out of the given options pick the one that gives
their correct order.
A. There are many gadgets that are operated by a remote control and contain a silicon chip.
B. This produces an infra-red beam, made up of electromagnetic waves.
C. When a button is pressed on the remote control, the chip sets off an electronic vibration.
D. The beam carries a coded signal for operating the systems.
Ans 1. ACDB
2. ACBD
3. BACD
4. ADCB

Q.3 Select the passive form of the given sentence.
People claim to have seen the wild and mad elephant in several cities.
Ans 1. The wild and mad elephant is claimed to have been seen in several cities.
2. The wild and mad elephant was claimed to be seen by people in several cities.
3. The wild and mad elephant has been claimed to be seen by the people in several
cities.
4. The wild and mad elephant is being claimed to be seen in several cities.

Q.1 Given below are four jumbled sentences. Out of the given options pick the one that gives
their correct order.
A. There are many gadgets that are operated by a remote control and contain a silicon chip.
B. This produces an infra-red beam, made up of electromagnetic waves.
C. When a button is pressed on the remote control, the chip sets off an electronic vibration.
D. The beam carries a coded signal for operating the systems.
Ans 1. ACDB
2. ACBD
3. BACD
4. ADCB

People claim to have seen the wild and mad elephant in several cities.
Ans 1. The wild and mad elephant is claimed to have been seen in several cities.
2. The wild and mad elephant was claimed to be seen by people in several cities.
3. The wild and mad elephant has been claimed to be seen by the people in several
cities.
4. The wild and mad elephant is being claimed to be seen in several cities.

Q.23 Select the correct passive form of the given sentence.
He incurred heavy losses in business.
Ans 1. Heavy losses are being incurred in business by him.
2. Heavy losses are incurred in business by him.
3. Heavy losses were incurred in business by him.
4. Heavy losses was incurred in business by him.
